<div id="review_620299278" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/620299278" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/620299278?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9780316193061" href="/book/show/12256500-beautiful-chaos">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=witches">witches</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer620299278" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3036133913964066562">Ever since Lena claimed herself to be both light and dark on the seventeenth moon, nothing is right in Gatlin, NC. The heat has scorched everything. The town is infested with a locust type insect called lubbers. They have earthquakes. Even the Castor's powers aren't working properly. Ethan keeps having strange dreams and he keeps forgetting things, small parts of himself, memories. But, Ethan is the Wayward. He has to find "The one who is two" because that is who can fix everything. Put the worl</span>
  <span id="freeText3036133913964066562" style="display:none">Ever since Lena claimed herself to be both light and dark on the seventeenth moon, nothing is right in Gatlin, NC. The heat has scorched everything. The town is infested with a locust type insect called lubbers. They have earthquakes. Even the Castor's powers aren't working properly. Ethan keeps having strange dreams and he keeps forgetting things, small parts of himself, memories. But, Ethan is the Wayward. He has to find "The one who is two" because that is who can fix everything. Put the world back in order. But who is it? <br /><br />First of all, I think that this is my favorite of this series so far. And a word of warning, it ends on a huge cliff hanger. Thank goodness I have the final book right here to start on as soon as I finish writing this. I can't say enough good things about who Ethan, Lena and yes, even Link, have become. I can feel the love between Ethan and Lena seeping off the pages into my own heart. Every time they touch or kiss, though, Lena has some sort of electrical charge and poor Ethan, his heart starts hammering and he almost passes out. But, they don't let this bother them. And the responsibility they carry on their shoulders. They are somehow trying to go to school and do the things other 17 year olds do but at the same time they are trying to save their town and all the people they love. And Link! I just love him. He is funny, quirky but at the same time, strong and loyal. He sticks by his best friend, Ethan, no matter what. <br /><br />There is one particular quote I wanted to put in this review that really sums up the kind of person Ethan has become: Your first kiss isn't as important as your last. The math test really didn't matter. The pie really did. The stuff you're good at and the stuff you're bad at are just different parts of the same thing. Same goes for the people you love and the people you don't - and the people who love you and the people who don't. The only thing that mattered was that you cared about a few people. Life is really, really short. <br /><br />I loved this book and can't wait to begin the final book, which I am going to do in about five minutes. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3036133913964066562" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_427583442" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/427583442" />
    <a title="Jenn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3957464-jenn"><img alt="Jenn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1360078699p2/3957464.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/427583442?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenn" href="/user/show/3957464-jenn">Jenn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12334378-beautiful-chaos">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=small-town-charm">small-town-charm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=3-star-reads">3-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=wordy-af">wordy-af</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=high-school-days">high-school-days</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3957464-jenn?shelf=paranormal-supernatural">paranormal-supernatural</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer427583442" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6353886243078528331">So far from the series, I think this may be my favorite one so far. But man, this was still wordy as all hell. <br/><br/>Lena has pretty much broken the world with her life choices. When she claimed herself, no one foresaw the ripples that would have on the universe. Now, it's pretty much apocalypse time and no one knows quite what to do - and on top of that, Ethan is experiencing some really weird changes within himself, but he doesn't tell anyone about them, choosing to try to figure it out on his own -</span>
  <span id="freeText6353886243078528331" style="display:none">So far from the series, I think this may be my favorite one so far. But man, this was still wordy as all hell. <br /><br />Lena has pretty much broken the world with her life choices. When she claimed herself, no one foresaw the ripples that would have on the universe. Now, it's pretty much apocalypse time and no one knows quite what to do - and on top of that, Ethan is experiencing some really weird changes within himself, but he doesn't tell anyone about them, choosing to try to figure it out on his own - typical teenage boy.<br /><br />There was a lot more Link in this one too, mostly due to the changes happening with him as well. I found him to be super annoying at times with his new powers - really only caring about how popular he was and how to make Ridley jealous. Because once again, no one talks to each other!<br /><br />But speaking of Ridley - <b>OMG I HATE EVERYTHING ABOUT HER!</b> All she does is whine whine whine and then be a bitch then whine whine whine some more. "I'm mortal. Poor me. I can't seduce men anymore. I have no powers. I hate Link. Why is Link with that person? Did I also tell you I'm mortal?" SHUT UP. I really hope to never see her again in this series or spinoffs because this is a character who is completely unredeemable to me. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I mean, she had herself turned into a dark caster by the very people who are trying to kill her family just because she doesn't want to be mortal anymore. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Morals, this girl's got them.<br /><br />A main issue I have with this series is how long the books are for no good reason. I feel like I have to wade through meaningless dialogue just to get to the actual plot. And speaking of plot, the main storyline didn't even really come into play until halfway through the book. So my three star rating is mostly due to the last 1/3 because that's when things actually start to happen. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6353886243078528331" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_169867141" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/169867141" />
    <a title="Aimee ♥ | Aimee, Always" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5478965-aimee-aimee-always"><img alt="Aimee ♥ | Aimee, Always" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1562987681p2/5478965.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/169867141?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aimee ♥ | Aimee, Always" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aimee ♥ | Aimee, Always" href="/user/show/5478965-aimee-aimee-always">Aimee ♥ | Aimee, Always</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5478965-aimee-aimee-always?shelf=covergasm">covergasm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5478965-aimee-aimee-always?shelf=ending-sucked">ending-sucked</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer169867141" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2750045517533933890">If I thought the first two <i>Caster Chronicles</i> books were good, <i>Beautiful Chaos</i> was awesome!<br/><br/>----<br/><br/><b>Synopsis:</b><br/>Ethan Wate thought he was getting used to the strange, impossible events happening in Gatlin, his small Southern town. But now that Ethan and Lena have returned home, strange and impossible have taken on new meanings. Swarms of locusts, record-breaking heat, and devastating storms ravage Gatlin as Ethan and Lena struggle to understand the impact of Lena's Claiming. Even Lena's family of powerfu</span>
  <span id="freeText2750045517533933890" style="display:none">If I thought the first two <i>Caster Chronicles</i> books were good, <i>Beautiful Chaos</i> was awesome!<br /><br />----<br /><br /><b>Synopsis:</b><br />Ethan Wate thought he was getting used to the strange, impossible events happening in Gatlin, his small Southern town. But now that Ethan and Lena have returned home, strange and impossible have taken on new meanings. Swarms of locusts, record-breaking heat, and devastating storms ravage Gatlin as Ethan and Lena struggle to understand the impact of Lena's Claiming. Even Lena's family of powerful Supernaturals is affected - and their abilities begin to dangerously misfire. As time passes, one question becomes clear: What - or who - will need to be sacrificed to save Gatlin?<br />For Ethan, the chaos is a frightening but welcome distraction. He's being haunted in his dreams again, but this time it isn't by Lena - and whatever is haunting him is following him out of his dreams and into his everyday life. Even worse, Ethan is gradually losing pieces of himself - forgetting names, phone numbers, even memories. He doesn't know why, and most days he's too afraid to ask.<br /><br />Sometimes there isn't just one answer or one choice. Sometimes there's no going back. And this time there won't be a happy ending.<br /><br />-----<br /><br />Honestly: I cried six times total throughout the book.<br /><br />When I first read the blurb and I saw the part that said "And this time there won't be a happy ending", my hopes of a fairy tale ending burned.<br /><br />Ridley was a really depressing character in this one. One of the scenes where I cried was when <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Ridley turned into a Dark Caster again. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Damn these twists!<br /><br />And surprisingly, the infamous John Breed returns! And guess what? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He's a good guy! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />This installment of the <i>Caster Chronicles</i> series really had twists and turns everytwhere. It was heartbreaking.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2750045517533933890" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('F2uxXa7GlBpxSIOiZXi+omFKxZ9lz5ZSp+nYvUhsMogtTdiPFZhdctZjN8OSjbR9txUiV6tCGDX8l54MhS/AEg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('sA6HT7pD1iDq6zAk300a9HjHSB6iN8Xw2HEDkSb77ICKKO6dAR0fSE3AhEUouBArrpiv1my6S5eDD0Ug67geGg==')})
  }
//]]>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2520419063804966925">Kami Garcia is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author. She is the coauthor of the BEAUTIFUL CREATURES series, which has been published in 51 countries and 37 languages, with over 10 million copies in print. In 2013, Beautiful Creatures released as a feature film from Warner Brothers. Kami is a cofounder of the YALLFEST kid lit book festival and the author of five solo</span>
  <span id="freeText2520419063804966925" style="display:none">Kami Garcia is a #1 New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author. She is the coauthor of the BEAUTIFUL CREATURES series, which has been published in 51 countries and 37 languages, with over 10 million copies in print. In 2013, Beautiful Creatures released as a feature film from Warner Brothers. Kami is a cofounder of the YALLFEST kid lit book festival and the author of five solo novels, including her Bram Stoker Award-nominated novels Unbreakable and Unmarked (THE LEGION series) and The X-Files Origins: Agent of Chaos. Kami’s first graphic novel Teen Titans: Raven, with artist Gabriel Picolo, is the first book in her TEEN TITANS series for DC Comics and the adult series JOKER/HARLEY: CRIMINAL SANITY, from DC Black Label.<br /><br />Find Kami online at kamigarcia.com, on Facebook @KamiGarciaYA, and on Twitter and Instagram @KamiGarcia. </span>
